Basic Website

SQL Query Results


Query 1: List the top 5 most reviewed products with average rating above 4.
Response 1:
SELECT r.product_id, AVG(r.rating) AS avg_rating, COUNT(r.id) AS review_count FROM reviews r GROUP BY r.product_id HAVING AVG(r.rating) > 4 ORDER BY review_count DESC LIMIT 5

[
    [
        "product_id",
        "avg_rating",
        "review_count"
    ],
    [
        [
            41,
            "62.0000",
            1
        ],
        [
            103,
            "25.0000",
            1
        ],
        [
            156,
            "72.0000",
            1
        ],
        [
            38,
            "61.0000",
            1
        ]
    ]
]


Query 2: Find all users who reviewed more than one product with "organic" in the title.
Response 2:
SELECT DISTINCT r.user_id, u.name, u.email FROM reviews r JOIN products p ON r.product_id = p.id JOIN users u ON r.user_id = u.id WHERE p.title LIKE '%organic%' GROUP BY r.user_id HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT r.product_id) > 1

[
    [
        "user_id",
        "name",
        "email"
    ],
    []
]


Query 3: Show the average rating per sub_category_id for b2c products.
Response 3:
SELECT AVG(r.rating) AS avg_rating, p.sub_category_id FROM reviews r JOIN products p ON r.product_id = p.id WHERE p.product_type = 'b2c' GROUP BY p.sub_category_id

[
    [
        "avg_rating",
        "sub_category_id"
    ],
    [
        [
            "61.0000",
            3
        ],
        [
            "62.0000",
            4
        ]
    ]
]


Query 4: List products reviewed by users from the same city as the product delivery area.
Response 4:
SELECT DISTINCT r.product_id FROM reviews AS r INNER JOIN addresses AS a ON r.city = a.city

[
    [
        "product_id"
    ],
    []
]


Query 5: Which products have b2c_price greater than b2b_price?
Response 5:

Query 9: Which products have the same value for b2c_price and b2c_sale_price?
Response 9:
SELECT id, main_category_id, sub_category_id, sku, title, description, delivery_time, free_pickup_store, product_type, b2c_price, b2c_sale_price, b2b_price, b2b_sale_price, b2b_min_quantity, gallery FROM products WHERE b2c_price = b2c_sale_price

Query 13: Which products have a higher discount percentage in b2b compared to b2c?
Response 13:
SELECT oi.product_title, (oi.price - ci.discounted_price) / oi.price * 100 AS discount_percentage FROM order_items oi INNER JOIN cart_items ci ON oi.product_id = ci.product_id WHERE oi.price > ci.discounted_price ORDER BY discount_percentage DESC

[
    [
        "product_title",
        "discount_percentage"
    ],
    []
]


Query 14: List products where b2b_price and b2c_price are both null.
Response 14:
SELECT p.* FROM products AS p WHERE p.b2b_price IS NULL AND p.b2c_price IS NULL

[
    [
        "id",
        "main_category_id",
        "sub_category_id",
        "sku",
        "title",
        "description",
        "delivery_time",

        "product_type",
        "b2c_price",
        "b2c_sale_price",
        "b2b_price",
        "b2b_sale_price",
        "b2b_min_quantity",
        "gallery",
        "created_at",
        "updated_at"
    ],
    []
]


Query 15: What is the average b2c_price across all products?
Response 15:
SELECT AVG(b2c_price) AS average_b2c_price FROM products

[
    [
        "average_b2c_price"
    ],
    [
        [
            "553.300976"
        ]
    ]
]


Query 16: What is the maximum b2b_sale_price in the database?
Response 16:
SELECT MAX(b2b_sale_price) AS max_b2b_sale_price FROM products

Query 17: List products where b2c_sale_price is at least 20% lower than b2c_price.
Response 17:
SELECT p.* FROM products p WHERE p.b2c_sale_price <= (p.b2c_price * 0.8)

Query 26: Which products have free pickup available and belong to a specific main_category_id?
Response 26:
SELECT p.* FROM products p JOIN jobs j ON p.id = j.id WHERE p.main_category_id = 1 AND j.available_at IS NOT NULL

[
    [
        "id",
        "main_category_id",
        "sub_category_id",
        "sku",
        "title",
        "description",
        "delivery_time",
        "free_pickup_store",
        "product_type",
        "b2c_price",
        "b2c_sale_price",
        "b2b_price",
        "b2b_sale_price",
        "b2b_min_quantity",
        "gallery",
        "created_at",
        "updated_at"
    ],
    []
]

Query 34: What is the average number of products added per month?
Response 34:
SELECT AVG(count) AS average_count FROM (SELECT COUNT(*) AS count, EXTRACT(MONTH FROM created_at) AS month, EXTRACT(YEAR FROM created_at) AS year FROM addresses GROUP BY EXTRACT(MONTH FROM created_at), EXTRACT(YEAR FROM created_at)) AS subquery

[
    [
        "average_count"
    ],

        [

Query 38: List all reviews for products with "eco-friendly" in the title.
Response 38:
SELECT r.id, r.rating, r.review, r.name, r.email, r.city, p.title AS product_title FROM reviews r JOIN products p ON r.product_id = p.id WHERE p.title LIKE '%eco-friendly%'

Query 45: List reviews created in the last 7 days for products in sub_category_id = 10.
Response 45:
SELECT r.id, r.rating, r.review, r.name, r.email, r.city, r.user_id, p.sub_category_id FROM reviews r INNER JOIN products p ON r.product_id = p.id WHERE p.sub_category_id = 10 AND r.created_at >= NOW() - INTERVAL 7 DAY

Query 48: List products that were reviewed within 3 days of being created.
Response 48:

Query 49: Find users who left a review within 24 hours of account creation.
Response 49:
SELECT u.* FROM users u JOIN reviews r ON u.id = r.user_id WHERE TIMESTAMPDIFF(HOUR, u.created_at, r.created_at) <= 24

Query 52: How many users have reviewed more than 5 products?
Response 52:
SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT r.user_id) AS total_users FROM reviews r WHERE r.user_id IN ( SELECT r2.user_id FROM reviews r2 GROUP BY r2.user_id HAVING COUNT(r2.product_id) > 5 )
